{\footnotesize\ttfamily def doxmlparser.\+index.\+Mixed\+Container.\+export\+Simple (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self,  }\item[{}]{outfile,  }\item[{}]{level,  }\item[{}]{name }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{00854     \textcolor{keyword}{def }exportSimple(self, outfile, level, name):}
\DoxyCodeLine{00855         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} self.content\_type == MixedContainer.TypeString:}
\DoxyCodeLine{00856             outfile.write(\textcolor{stringliteral}{'<\%s>\%s</\%s>'} \% (}
\DoxyCodeLine{00857                 self.name, self.value, self.name))}
\DoxyCodeLine{00858         \textcolor{keywordflow}{elif} self.content\_type == MixedContainer.TypeInteger \textcolor{keywordflow}{or} \(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{00859                 self.content\_type == MixedContainer.TypeBoolean:}
\DoxyCodeLine{00860             outfile.write(\textcolor{stringliteral}{'<\%s>\%d</\%s>'} \% (}
\DoxyCodeLine{00861                 self.name, self.value, self.name))}
\DoxyCodeLine{00862         \textcolor{keywordflow}{elif} self.content\_type == MixedContainer.TypeFloat \textcolor{keywordflow}{or} \(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{00863                 self.content\_type == MixedContainer.TypeDecimal:}
\DoxyCodeLine{00864             outfile.write(\textcolor{stringliteral}{'<\%s>\%f</\%s>'} \% (}
\DoxyCodeLine{00865                 self.name, self.value, self.name))}
\DoxyCodeLine{00866         \textcolor{keywordflow}{elif} self.content\_type == MixedContainer.TypeDouble:}
\DoxyCodeLine{00867             outfile.write(\textcolor{stringliteral}{'<\%s>\%g</\%s>'} \% (}
\DoxyCodeLine{00868                 self.name, self.value, self.name))}
\DoxyCodeLine{00869         \textcolor{keywordflow}{elif} self.content\_type == MixedContainer.TypeBase64:}
\DoxyCodeLine{00870             outfile.write(\textcolor{stringliteral}{'<\%s>\%s</\%s>'} \% (}
\DoxyCodeLine{00871                 self.name,}
\DoxyCodeLine{00872                 base64.b64encode(self.value),}
\DoxyCodeLine{00873                 self.name))}

\DoxyCodeLine{00859                 self.content\_type == MixedContainer.TypeBoolean:}

\DoxyCodeLine{00862         \textcolor{keywordflow}{elif} self.content\_type == MixedContainer.TypeFloat \textcolor{keywordflow}{or} \(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{00863                 self.content\_type == MixedContainer.TypeDecimal:}
\DoxyCodeLine{00864             outfile.write(\textcolor{stringliteral}{'<\%s>\%f</\%s>'} \% (}

\DoxyCodeLine{00866         \textcolor{keywordflow}{elif} self.content\_type == MixedContainer.TypeDouble:}

\DoxyCodeLine{00875         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} self.category == MixedContainer.CategoryText:}
\DoxyCodeLine{00876             \textcolor{comment}{\# Prevent exporting empty content as empty lines.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00877             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} self.value.strip():}
\DoxyCodeLine{00878                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} \mbox{\hyperlink{build_2doxygen_2libmscgen_2gd_8h_afed088663f8704004425cdae2120b9b3}{len}}(element) > 0:}

\DoxyCodeLine{00880                         element[-\/1].tail = self.value}
\DoxyCodeLine{00881                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}:}

\DoxyCodeLine{00883                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{00884                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} element.text \textcolor{keywordflow}{is} \textcolor{keywordtype}{None}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{00885                         element.text = self.value}
\DoxyCodeLine{00886                     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{00887                         element.text += self.value}
\DoxyCodeLine{00888         \textcolor{keywordflow}{elif} self.category == MixedContainer.CategorySimple:}
\DoxyCodeLine{00889             subelement = etree\_.SubElement(}
\DoxyCodeLine{00890                 element, \textcolor{stringliteral}{'\%s'} \% self.name)}
\DoxyCodeLine{00891             subelement.text = self.to\_etree\_simple()}
\DoxyCodeLine{00892         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}:    \textcolor{comment}{\# category == MixedContainer.CategoryComplex}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00893             self.value.to\_etree(element)}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{to\_etree\_simple()}{to\_etree\_simple()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily def doxmlparser.\+index.\+Mixed\+Container.\+to\+\_\+etree\+\_\+simple (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{self,  }\item[{}]{mapping\+\_\+ = {\ttfamily None},  }\item[{}]{nsmap\+\_\+ = {\ttfamily None} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{addon_2doxmlparser_2doxmlparser_2index_8py_source_l00894}{894}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{addon_2doxmlparser_2doxmlparser_2index_8py_source}{index.\+py}}.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{00894     \textcolor{keyword}{def }to\_etree\_simple(self, mapping\_=None, nsmap\_=None):}
\DoxyCodeLine{00895         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} self.content\_type == MixedContainer.TypeString:}
\DoxyCodeLine{00896             text = self.value}
\DoxyCodeLine{00897         \textcolor{keywordflow}{elif} (self.content\_type == MixedContainer.TypeInteger \textcolor{keywordflow}{or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00898                 self.content\_type == MixedContainer.TypeBoolean):}
\DoxyCodeLine{00899             text = \textcolor{stringliteral}{'\%d'} \% self.value}
\DoxyCodeLine{00900         \textcolor{keywordflow}{elif} (self.content\_type == MixedContainer.TypeFloat \textcolor{keywordflow}{or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00901                 self.content\_type == MixedContainer.TypeDecimal):}
\DoxyCodeLine{00902             text = \textcolor{stringliteral}{'\%f'} \% self.value}
\DoxyCodeLine{00903         \textcolor{keywordflow}{elif} self.content\_type == MixedContainer.TypeDouble:}
\DoxyCodeLine{00904             text = \textcolor{stringliteral}{'\%g'} \% self.value}
\DoxyCodeLine{00905         \textcolor{keywordflow}{elif} self.content\_type == MixedContainer.TypeBase64:}
\DoxyCodeLine{00906             text = \textcolor{stringliteral}{'\%s'} \% base64.b64encode(self.value)}
\DoxyCodeLine{00907         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} text}

\end{DoxyCode}
